Tembo Global Industries Limited    TEMBO : Outcome of Board Meeting Sub: Outcome of Board Meeting held on 22nd , December, 2020

The Board of Directors of the company considered and approved the following proposal:-

1.	Considered and discussed and approved the Loan agreement of Rs. 2500000/- (Rupees Twenty Five Lakhs only) to the Subsidiary M/S Saketh Seven Star Industries Limited.
2.	Considered and authorized Mr. Sanjay Jashbhai Patel Managing Director of the Company be to take all necessary steps relating to grant of loan to M/s. Aster DM Healthcare Limited    ASTERDM : Updates ASTERDM : Aster DM Healthcare Limited has informed the Exchange regarding 'signing of an agreement with the Government of the Cayman Islands for setting up Healthcare and related services in the Cayman Islands.

With reference to the captioned subject, we would like to inform that Aster DM Healthcare Limited ( the Company ) through its subsidiary company, Aster Caribbean Holdings Ltd has entered into an agreement with the Cayman Islands Government to further a healthcare project in the Cayman Islands to be known as the  Aster Cayman Medcity  for the provision of healthcare services.

The agreement will see Aster initially develop a 150-bed comprehensive, tertiary and quaternary hospital, alongside an assisted living facility and healthcare university in the long-term, as part of a joint commitment to seeing the Cayman Islands develop as THE destination for Destination Healthcare, or medical tourism.

The details required as per Circular Number CIR/CFD/CMD/4/2015 dated September 09, 2015 pertaining to continuous disclosure requirements for Listed Entities under Regulation 30 of Securities and Exchange Board of India (Listing Obligations and Disclosure Requirements) Regulations, 2015, has been enclosed as Annexure I'.
